    \begin{tikzpicture}[>=stealth',shorten >= 1pt,auto,node distance=1.4cm,semithick, state/.style={circle,draw,minimum size=0.5cm,inner sep=0pt}]

    \node[state]         (q0)                                                       {0};
    \node                               (q0a)   [right of=q0]                       {};
    \node                               (q0b)   [right of=q0a]                      {};
    \node                               (q0c)   [right of=q0b]                      {};
    \node[state]        (q1)    [right of=q0c]                      {2};
    \node[state]        (q2)    [below of=q0]                       {3};
    \node                               (q2a)   [right of=q2]                       {};
    \node                               (q2b)   [right of=q2a]                      {};
    \node                               (q2c)   [right of=q2b]                      {};
    \node[state]        (q3)    [below of=q1]                       {3};
    \node[state]         (q4)    [above=1.4cm of q0a]                {3};
    \node[state]        (q5)    [below of=q2a]                      {3};
    \node                               (q6a)   [above of=q0b]                      {};
    \node[state]         (q6)    [above of=q6a]                      {1};
    \node                               (q7a)   [below of=q2b]                      {};
    \node[state]        (q7)    [below of=q7a]                      {1};
    \node[state]         (q8)    [above of=q0c]                      {1};
    \node[state]         (q9)    [below=1.6cm of q2c]                {1};
    \node                               (q10a)  [above of=q0]                       {};
    \node[state]       (q10)   [above left =2cm of q10a]               {0};
    \node                               (q11a)  [below of=q2]                       {};
    \node[state]      (q11)   [below=2.5cm of q11a]               {2};
    \node                              (q0e1)    [right of=q1]                      {};
    \node[state]                       (q011)    [right of=q0e1]                      {0};
    \node[state]                       (q111)    [right of=q011]                      {1};
    \node[state]                       (q211)    [below of=q111]                      {2};
    \node[state]                       (q311)    [below of=q011]                      {3};

    \path[->]
                (q0) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q1)
                (q0) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q2)
                (q0) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q3)
                (q1) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q4)
                (q1) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q5)
                (q2) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q6)
                (q2) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q7)
                (q3) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q8)
                (q3) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q9)
                (q4) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q6)
                (q4) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q8)
                (q5) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q7)
                (q5) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q9)
                (q6) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q10)
                (q7) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q11)
                (q8) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q11)
                (q9) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q10)
                (q10) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q11)
                ;
    \path[->]
                (q011) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q211)
                (q011) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q311)
                (q111) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q011)
                (q111) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q211)
                (q211) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q311)
                (q311) edge [sloped, above]		node [align=center]	{}	(q111)
                ;
    \end{tikzpicture}
